# FBA REPORT VALIDATION ANALYSIS

**Generated:** 2025-12-30 12:00 UTC+04:00  
**Source Dataset:** `part_30_dec.xlsx` (2102 rows)  
**Reports Analyzed:** 8 (`cli`, `Codex HIGH`, `Codex samecha`, `Codex very high`, `Gemini`, `Opus`, `opus2`, `webapp gpt`)  

## Executive Summary

- **Scope analyzed:** 1268 report entries across 8 reports; **1214** entries were successfully mapped to the source dataset; **54** entries are **UNVERIFIABLE** due to ambiguous or missing mapping signals (RowID/ASIN/EAN/title collisions).
- **Overall accuracy (correct only):** **57.8%** (702/1214).  
  **Overall accuracy (correct+acceptable):** **80.1%** (973/1214).
- **Best performers (correct-only, comparable rows):** `webapp gpt` (**72.6%**), `cli` (**69.6%**), `Codex HIGH` (**65.4%**).  
  **Caveat:** `cli` covers **79 mapped rows** only and appears supplier-subset scoped; treat it as a **small-sample** indicator rather than a full-run benchmark.
- **Primary failure mode across models:** **Weak match overclassification** (claiming VERIFIED/HL/NV when the source titles/brand/type evidence does not meet the stated thresholds).

## Methodology

This validation follows your stated rule set (EAN matching, KNOWN_BRANDS brand confirmation, title similarity thresholds, pack-count and variant checks, profitability gates).  
For every extracted report row, I:

1. **Mapped the report row to the source dataset** using a precedence of (validated RowID) → ASIN/EAN/EAN_OnPage → title similarity scoring.  
   - If mapping could not be established with adequate confidence, the row is labeled **UNVERIFIABLE**.
2. **Computed an independent classification** from the source row only (not trusting report fields), including:
   - EAN match (normalized GTIN equivalence)
   - Brand match (KNOWN_BRANDS in both titles)
   - Title similarity (sequence similarity)
   - Pack ratio + adjusted profit (per your formula where applicable)
   - Variant mismatch (scent/color/size/capacity keywords)
3. **Scored the AI category vs. the independent category**:
   - **CORRECT**: exact match
   - **ACCEPTABLE**: adjacent category per your rubric (e.g., HL ↔ NV)
   - **INCORRECT**: materially wrong category assignment

## Recommendations

1. **For production use (balanced precision/recall):** prioritize `webapp gpt` or `Codex HIGH` as the primary generator; they exhibit the strongest **correct-only** performance across a non-trivial volume of mapped rows.
2. **For conservative shortlisting:** `opus2` shows a high **correct+acceptable** rate, but a lower correct-only rate; it is suitable if you prefer fewer “hard commits” and are comfortable reviewing NV/adjacent calls.
3. **For calibration work:** `Codex very high` underperforms materially on correct-only accuracy in this dataset; use it only if its configuration is being actively tuned and re-validated.

## Deliverables Exported

- `validation_entries_full.csv` — full per-entry evaluation (all 8 reports, untruncated)  
- `validation_ground_truth_unique_products.csv` — unique source rows referenced across reports + independent classification (untruncated)
